          </object>
         </h3>
        </div>
       </a>
      </li>
     </ul>

         <div class="category-type-background">
          <h4>
           <span>
            Architecture
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/architecture/">
           Architecture
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/tres-birds-wraps-wisconsins-art-preserve-in-slanted-strips-of-fir-wood/">
           Tres Birds wraps Wisconsin's Art Preserve in slanted strips of fir wood
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Work by self-taught artists will be displayed within a
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/douglas-fir/">
          Douglas fir
         </a>
         -wrapped
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/museums/">
          museum
         </a>
         in eastern
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/wisconsin/">
          Wisconsin
         </a>
         designed by US firm Tres Birds Workshop to evoke the natural landscape.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/tres-birds-wraps-wisconsins-art-preserve-in-slanted-strips-of-fir-wood/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <div class="category-type-background">
          <h4>
           <span>
            The Mindcraft Project 2021
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/the-mindcraft-project-2021/">
           The Mindcraft Project 2021
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/kasper-kjeldgaard-wire-suspense-light-mindcraft-project/">
           Kasper Kjeldgaard makes electrical wire into sculptural Suspense light
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         A desire to create poetic compositions led to designer Kasper Kjeldgaard's delicate-looking Suspense light, featured as part of our
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/the-mindcraft-project-2021">
          Dezeen x The Mindcraft Project 2021
         </a>
         collaboration.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/kasper-kjeldgaard-wire-suspense-light-mindcraft-project/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/lovers-house-isla-architects-mallorcan-holiday-home/">
           Holes and windows create "abstract composition" on facades of Mallorcan holiday home
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Large openings frame views of the
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/swimming-pools/">
          swimming pool
         </a>
         and surrounding landscape from the living spaces and terraces of this
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/holiday-homes/">
          holiday home
         </a>
         on the island of
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/mallorca/">
          Mallorca
         </a>
         , designed by local studio Isla Architects.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/lovers-house-isla-architects-mallorcan-holiday-home/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Jean-Philippe Vassal, along with his
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/lacaton-vassal/">
          Lacaton &amp; Vassal
         </a>
         co-founder Anne Lacaton,
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/16/anne-lacaton-jean-philippe-vassal-pritzker-architecture-prize-2021/">
          won the Pritzker Architecture Prize earlier this week
         </a>
         . In this lecture, he explains the ideology behind the studio's work.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/pritzker-architecture-prize-winner-jean-philippe-vassal-royal-academy-lecture/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>
        <footer>

          Tom Ravenscroft

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/20/eleven-stylish-home-office-working-spaces-complement-decor-lookbook/">
           Eleven stylish home-working spaces that complement the decor
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/home-offices/">
          Home offices
         </a>
         don't have to look like work offices. For this
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/lookbooks/">
          lookbook
         </a>
         , we've rounded up eleven remote workspaces that don't compromise on style.

         </a>

         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">

           Interiors
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/blockstudio-apartment-basta-moscow-interior/">
           Blockstudio creates Parisian ambience in Moscow apartment
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Russian practice Blockstudio has mixed different materials, textures and time periods within this new-build Moscow
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/apartments/">
          apartment
         </a>
         to create the feeling of a lived-in Parisian
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/interiors/">
          interior
         </a>
         .
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/blockstudio-apartment-basta-moscow-interior/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/eucalyptus-house-paritzki-liani-architects-tree/">
           Eucalyptus tree slots into facade of Tel Aviv house by Paritzki &amp; Liani Architects
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Israeli studio
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/paritzki-and-liani-architects/">
          Paritzki &amp; Liani Architects
         </a>
         has left an opening in the facade of its latest project, Eucalyptus House, to create space for an old tree.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/21/eucalyptus-house-paritzki-liani-architects-tree/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/20/roth-sheppard-inserts-unexpected-elements-into-hapa-sushi-restaurant/">
           Roth Sheppard inserts unexpected elements into Hapa Sushi restaurant
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Chunky wooden partitions and distinctive
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/lighting/">
          lighting
         </a>
         fixtures feature in a Japanese
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/restaurants/">
          restaurant
         </a>
         in Denver designed by
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/roth-sheppard/">
          Roth Sheppard Architects
         </a>
         to offer "flashes of unanticipated excitement".
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/20/roth-sheppard-inserts-unexpected-elements-into-hapa-sushi-restaurant/">

         </a>

         <div class="category-type-background">
          <h4>
           <span>
            The Mindcraft Project 2021
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/the-mindcraft-project-2021/">
           The Mindcraft Project 2021
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/20/300kg-beauty-bath-frederik-nystrup-larsen-oliver-sundqvist-mindcraft-project/">
           Birds can enjoy 300kg Beauty Bath by Frederik Nystrup-Larsen and Oliver Sundqvist
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         A 300-kilogram aluminium sculpture contains one centimetre of water for a birdbath in Danish artists Frederik Nystrup-Larsen and Oliver Sundqvist's work, showcased in our
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/the-mindcraft-project-2021">
          Dezeen x The Mindcraft Project 2021
         </a>
         collaboration.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/20/300kg-beauty-bath-frederik-nystrup-larsen-oliver-sundqvist-mindcraft-project/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

          Dezeen staff

          20 March 2021
         </time>

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/kua-bay-residence-walker-warner-architects-house-hawaii/">
           Hawaii house by Walker Warner Architects hugged by volcanic rock
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         American firm
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/walker-warner-architects/">
          Walker Warner Architects
         </a>
         has perched a
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/basalt/">
          basalt
         </a>
         and
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/cedar/">
          cedar
         </a>
         -clad holidayÂ home in
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/hawaii/">
          Hawaii
         </a>
         on a mountainside of lava rock with an
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/infinity-pools/">
          infinity pool
         </a>
         that looks towards the sea.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/kua-bay-residence-walker-warner-architects-house-hawaii/">
          More
         </a>

         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/20/2hien-house-vietnam-cta-recycled-scallop-tiles/">
           2HIEN house in Vietnam built using tiles salvaged from the owners' previous home
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Vietnamese studio
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/cta">
          CTA
         </a>
         has unveiled a
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/houses/">
          house
         </a>
         clad with scallop
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/tiles/">
          tiles
         </a>
         , which were preserved by the owners when their old home was pulled down.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/20/2hien-house-vietnam-cta-recycled-scallop-tiles/">
          More
         </a>

          <h4>
           <span>
            Interiors
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/interiors/">
           Interiors
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/tattoo-studio-atelier-eva-williamsburg-new-york-interiors/">
           Williamsburg tattoo parlour Atelier Eva is designed to feel like a spa
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Turkish artist Eva Karabudak designed a soothing and welcoming interior for her
         <a href="http://dezeen.com/tag/tattoo-parlours">
          tattoo parlour
         </a>
         , Atelier Eva, in New York's
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/williamsburg">
          Williamsburg
         </a>
         neighbourhood.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/tattoo-studio-atelier-eva-williamsburg-new-york-interiors/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <div class="category-type-background">
          <h4>
           <span>
            Dezeen Showroom
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/showroom/">
           Dezeen Showroom
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/dezeen-showroom-pedrali-takt-andtradition-vondom-vank-flokk-roda-cuero-design/">
           Pedrali, &amp;tradition, Vondom and Takt showcase products on Dezeen Showroom
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Italian brand
         <a href="http://www.dezeen.com/showroom/pedrali">
          Pedrali
         </a>
         , Danish brand
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/showroom/andtradition/">
          &amp;tradition
         </a>
         , design brand
         <a href="http://www.dezeen.com/showroom/vondom">
          Vondom
         </a>
         and Danish furniture brand
         <a href="http://www.dezeen.com/showroom/takt">
          Takt
         </a>
         are among brands showcasing products on
         <a href="http://www.dezeen.com/showroom">
          Dezeen Showroom
         </a>
         this week.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/dezeen-showroom-pedrali-takt-andtradition-vondom-vank-flokk-roda-cuero-design/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

          <h4>
           <span>
            Roundups
           </span>

         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/roundups/">
           Roundups
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/17/key-projects-anne-lacaton-jean-philippe-vassal-pritzker-prize/">
           Ten key projects by Pritzker Architecture Prize-winners Anne Lacaton and Jean-Philippe Vassal
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Here are 10 key projects by French architect duo
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/lacaton-vassal/">
          Anne Lacaton and Jean-Philippe Vassal
         </a>
         , who have been named
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/16/anne-lacaton-jean-philippe-vassal-pritzker-architecture-prize-2021/">
          this year's laureates of the prestigious Pritzker Architecture Prize
         </a>
         .
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/17/key-projects-anne-lacaton-jean-philippe-vassal-pritzker-prize/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <div class="category-type-background">
          <h4>
           <span>
            Interview
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/features/interviews/">
           Interview
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/jean-philippe-vassal-pritzker-prize-interview/">
           "Generosity is absolutely essential in any act of architecture" says Jean-Philippe Vassal
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         In this previously unpublished interview,
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/lacaton-vassal/">
          Lacaton &amp; Vassal
         </a>
         co-founder Jean-Philippe Vassal explained why the
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/pritzker-prize/">
          2021 Pritzker Architecture Prize-winning studio
         </a>
         believes that buildings should be renovated instead of demolished.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/jean-philippe-vassal-pritzker-prize-interview/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <div class="category-type-background">
          <h4>
           <span>
            The Mindcraft Project 2021
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/the-mindcraft-project-2021/">
           The Mindcraft Project 2021
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/else-rikke-bruun-textile-veneer-screen-mindcraft-project/">
           Else-Rikke Bruun weaves flexible Textile Veneer screen from wood
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Danish designer Else-Rikke Bruun blurs the line between fabric and wood with her Textile Veneer screen, highlighted as part of our
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/the-mindcraft-project-2021">
          Dezeen x The Mindcraft Project 2021
         </a>
         collaboration.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/else-rikke-bruun-textile-veneer-screen-mindcraft-project/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/architecture/">
           Architecture
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/em-estudio-concrete-holiday-home-oaxaca/">
           Em-Estudio builds concrete holiday home on Oaxaca hillside
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Em-Estudio has built a
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/holiday-homes/">
          holiday home
         </a>
         on a steep hillside in Oaxaca,
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/mexico/">
          Mexico
         </a>
         , from
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/coloured-concrete/">
          coloured concrete
         </a>
         chosen to blend into the rocky mountainside.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/em-estudio-concrete-holiday-home-oaxaca/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

          <h4>
           <span>
            Office architecture
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/office-architecture/">
           Office architecture
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/carlsberg-hq-by-cf-moller-architects-copenhagen/">
           CF MÃ¸ller Architects designs Carlsberg HQ clad in recycled copper
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/c-f-moller/">
          CF MÃ¸ller Architects
         </a>
         has created a headquarters for Carlsberg Group in
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/copenhagen/">
          Copenhagen
         </a>
         with a recycled
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/copper/">
          copper
         </a>
         facade and a golden metal bridge to reference beer and brewing equipment.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/carlsberg-hq-by-cf-moller-architects-copenhagen/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <div class="category-type-background">
          <h4>
           <span>
            Design
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/design/">
           Design
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/17/allen-key-light-ikea-gelchop-art-event/">
           IKEA unveils Allen key lamp in homage to "the most iconic IKEA item of all"
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Japanese design studio Gelchop has created a
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/lamps/">
          lamp
         </a>
         for
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/ikea/">
          IKEA
         </a>
         that takes the shape of an oversized Allen key in a nod to the company's
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/flat-pack-furniture/">
          flat-pack furniture
         </a>
         legacy.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/17/allen-key-light-ikea-gelchop-art-event/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/virtual-25-gucci-wanna-digital-sneaker/">
           Gucci releases first virtual sneaker that can only be worn in digital environments
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/gucci/">
          Gucci
         </a>
         creative director Alessandro Michele has designed a pair of neon-coloured, digital-only
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/trainers/">
          trainers
         </a>
         that people can try on using
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/augmented-reality/">
          augmented reality
         </a>
         and "wear" in photographs for social media.

         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/specifying-tropical-timber-key-role-climate-change-battle-timber-trade-federation/">
           Specifying tropical timber can "play a key role in the climate change battle" says Timber Trade Federation
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Architects can help fight
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/climate-change/">
          climate change
         </a>
         by specifying tropical timber, according to
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/timber-trade-federation/">
          Timber Trade Federation
         </a>
         CEO David Hopkins.

          <h4>
           <span>
            Architecture
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/architecture/">
           Architecture
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/atelier-van-lieshout-cultural-neighbourhood-brutus-rotterdam-harbour/">
           Atelier Van Lieshout designs Brutus neighbourhood for artists in Rotterdam
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Artist
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/atelier-van-lieshout/">
          Joep van Lieshout
         </a>
         has designed a
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/brutalism/">
          brutalist
         </a>
         -informed residential neighbourhood and a cluster of cultural buildings in
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/rotterdam/">
          Rotterdam
         </a>
         as a "new model for urban renewal" that aims to foster an artistic community.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/atelier-van-lieshout-cultural-neighbourhood-brutus-rotterdam-harbour/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

          <h4>
           <span>
            Design
           </span>
          </h4>
         </div>
         <h4 class="category-type-foreground">
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/design/">
           Design
          </a>
         </h4>
         <h3>
          <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/heatherwick-studio-electric-car-im-motors/">
           Sketches reveal concept for Heatherwick Studio's electric car
          </a>
         </h3>
        </header>
        <p>
         Dezeen can reveal a pair of sketches that show the concept for an
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/electric-cars/">
          electric car
         </a>
         and
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/electric-vehicle-charging-stations/">
          charging station
         </a>
         that
         <a href="https://www.dezeen.com/tag/thomas-heatherwick/">
          Heatherwick Studio
         </a>
         is designing for newly formed Chinese car brand IM Motors.
         <a class="more-link" href="https://www.dezeen.com/2021/03/19/heatherwick-studio-electric-car-im-motors/">
          More
         </a>
        </p>

          Tom Ravenscroft

     <div class="dz-widget-wrap keyline">
      <div class="dzn-widget dzn-widget-jobs">
       <div class="dzn-widget-tabs cf">
        <h2>
         <a data-count="5" data-feed="//services.dezeen.com/jobs.recent.json" data-random="true">
          Popular jobs
         </a>
        </h2>
        <h2>
         <a data-feed="//services.dezeen.com/jobs.featured.json">
          Featured jobs
         </a>
        </h2>
       </div>
       <div class="dzn-widget-image">
       </div>
       <div class="dzn-widget-feeds">
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <script>
      if($('.dzn-widget').length > 0) {

        //INIT FEEDS
        $.each($('.dzn-widget-tabs'), initWidget);

        //EVENTS
        $('.dzn-widget .dzn-widget-tabs a').on('click', function (e){

            e.preventDefault();

            var parent_div  = $(this).closest('.dzn-widget');
            var tab_id      = $(this).closest('h2').data('tab');

            $('h2', parent_div).removeClass('active');
            $('h2[data-tab="' + tab_id + '"]', parent_div).addClass('active');

            $('.dzn-widget-feeds div', parent_div).removeClass('active');
            $('.dzn-widget-feeds div[data-tab="' + tab_id + '"]', parent_div).addClass('active');

        });

        $('.dzn-widget .dzn-widget-feeds').on('mouseenter', 'a', function (e) {

            e.preventDefault();
            var parent_div  = $(this).closest('.dzn-widget');
            $('img', parent_div).attr('src', $(this).parent('li').data('image')).attr('alt', $(this).text());

        });

        //GA TRACKING
        $('.dzn-widget .dzn-widget-feeds').on('click', 'a', function (e) {

            ga('send', 'event', 'list', 'widget', this.href);

        });

    }

    function initWidget(keyx, valuex) {

        var unique_widget_id = keyx; //Because there's a chance there's an identical widget elsewhere on the page

        $('h2', this).each(function(tab_id, valuey) {

            $(this).attr("data-tab", tab_id);

            if(tab_id == 0) {

                $(this).addClass('active');

            }

            var feed_a      = $('a', this);
            var feed_url    = feed_a.data('feed');
            var feed_count  = feed_a.data('count') == undefined ? 5 : feed_a.data('count');
            var feed_random = feed_a.data('random');

            $.getJSON( feed_url, function( data ) {

                var items           = [];
                var images          = [];
                var item_counter    = 1;
                var tracking        = '';

                if(feed_random == true) {

                    // From https://css-tricks.com/snippets/javascript/shuffle-array/
                    data.sort(function() { return 0.5 - Math.random() });

                }

                $.each( data, function( keyz, valz ) {

                    if(tab_id == 0 && item_counter == 1) {

                        valz.image
                        $( "<img>", {
                            "src": valz.image,
                            "alt" : valz.title,
                        }).appendTo( $('.dzn-widget-image', feed_a.closest('.dzn-widget')) );

                    }

                    if (tab_id == 0) {
                        tracking = '?utm_source=Dezeen%20Jobs%20widget&utm_medium=widget&utm_campaign=top%20jobs';
                    } else {
                        tracking = '?utm_source=Dezeen%20Jobs%20widget&utm_medium=widget&utm_campaign=featured%20jobs';
                    }                    

                    items.push("<li data-image='" + valz.image + "'><span>" + item_counter + "</span><a href='" + valz.permalink + tracking + "'>" + valz.title + "</a></li>");

                    item_counter++;

                    if(item_counter > feed_count) {

                         return false;

                    }

                });

                $( "<div/>", {
                    "class": (tab_id == 0 ? 'active' : ''),
                    "data-tab" : tab_id,
                    html: '<ol>' + items.join( "" ) + '</ol>'
                }).appendTo( $('.dzn-widget-feeds', feed_a.closest('.dzn-widget')) );

            });

        });

    }
     </script>

  <script>
   // Set the ago text on articles if withing 24 hrs of publish time

    jQuery.get('/yesterday.txt', function (data) {

        jQuery('.main-story-list time').each(function () {

            data_split = data.split(',');

            if ($(this).data('published') > data_split[0]) {

                $(this).html(timeSince($(this).data('published'), data_split[1]) + ' ago');

            }

        });

        jQuery('.single time').each(function () { // for article pages where time is in an a tag

            data_split = data.split(',');

            if ($(this).data('published') > data_split[0]) {

                $(this).find('a').html(timeSince($(this).data('published'), data_split[1]) + ' ago');

            }

        });

    });

    //AW: Nicked from here http://stackoverflow.com/a/3177838
    function timeSince(date, now) {

        var seconds = Math.floor((now - date));

        interval = Math.floor(seconds / 3600);

        if (interval > 1) {
            return interval + " hours";
        }

        if (interval == 1) {
            return interval + " hour";
        }
        //HELLO
        interval = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
        if (interval > 1) {
            return interval + " minutes";
        }
        return Math.floor(seconds) + " seconds";
    }
  </script>
